CREATE TABLE [dbo].[DomainUser](
	[id] [int] IDENTITY(1000,1) NOT NULL,
	[sn] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[distinguishedName] [nvarchar](128) NULL,
	[sAMAccountName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[mail] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[title] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[telephoneNumber] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[whenCreated] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[whenChanged] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[proxyAddress] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[physicalDeliveryOfficeName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[name] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[mailNickname] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[givenName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[cn] [nvarchar](128) NULL,
	[company] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[userAccountControl] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[msExchUserCulture] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[department] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[displayName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[description] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[userPrincipalName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[userRole] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[userGroup] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[objectGUID] [nvarchar](256) NULL,
	[temp2] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[temp3] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[temp4] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[temp5] [nvarchar](50) NULL
) ON [PRIMARY]

GO
